/* ===================================================
TEXT ANIMATION
=================================================== */ 

.text-to-animate {
  display: inline-block;
  visibility: hidden; /* Initially hide the entire text */
}


.text-to-animate span.outer {
  display: inline-block;
  overflow: hidden; /* Clipping the text here */
}

.text-to-animate span.inner {
  display: inline-block;
  will-change: transform; /* Optimizing animation performance */
  padding-bottom: 3px;
  margin-top: -3px;
}

/* Initially hide the entire text block */
.text-to-animate {
  visibility: hidden; /* Keeps the text hidden until the GSAP animation starts */
}

/* Outer span to clip the text and ensure overflow is hidden */
.outer {
  display: inline-block; /* Ensure .outer wraps the words properly */
  overflow: hidden;      /* Clip the content inside .inner */
  vertical-align: bottom; /* Align inline-block elements vertically */
}

/* Inner span that will be animated */
.inner {
  display: inline-block;    /* Allow smooth animation for the content inside */
  visibility: hidden;        /* Hide it initially */
}

    /********** Range Input Styles **********/
/*Range Reset*/
input[type="range"] {
   -webkit-appearance: none;
    appearance: none;
    background: transparent;
    cursor: pointer;

    transform-origin: 50% 50%;
    writing-mode: vertical-lr;
    direction: rtl;
    appearance: slider-vertical;
}

/* Removes default focus */
input[type="range"]:focus {
  outline: none;
}

input[type="range"]::slider-thumb {
   background-color: white;
   border:2px solid currentColor;
   height: 20px;
   width: 20px;
   transform:scale(1.5);
    
}

/***** Chrome, Safari, Opera and Edge Chromium styles *****/
/* slider track */
input[type="range"]::-webkit-slider-runnable-track {
   background-color: currentColor;
   border-radius: 0.5rem;
   height: 3px;
}

/* slider thumb */
input[type="range"]::-webkit-slider-thumb {
  -webkit-appearance: none; /* Override default look */
   appearance: none;
   margin-top: -12px; /* Centers thumb on the track */

   /*custom styles*/
   background-color: white;
   border:2px solid currentColor;
   height: 20px;
   width: 20px;
   transform:scale(1.5);
}

input[type="range"]:focus::-webkit-slider-thumb {   
  /* border: 1px solid orange;
  outline: 3px solid orange;
  outline-offset: 0.125rem; */
}

/******** Firefox styles ********/
/* slider track */
input[type="range"]::-moz-range-track {
   background-color: currentColor;
   border-radius: 0.5rem;
   height: 3px;
}

/* slider thumb */
input[type="range"]::-moz-range-thumb {
   border: none; /*Removes extra border that FF applies*/
   border-radius: 0; /*Removes default border-radius that FF applies*/

   /*custom styles*/
   background-color: white;
   border:2px solid currentColor;
   height: 20px;
   width: 20px;
}

input[type="range"]:focus::-moz-range-thumb {
  /* border: 1px solid orange;
  outline: 3px solid orange;
  outline-offset: 0.125rem;  */
}


:root {
    --range-slider-border: 1px;
    --range-slider-width: 8px;
}
@media all and (min-width:1100px) {
    :root {
        --range-slider-border: 2px;
        --range-slider-width: 16px;
    } 
}

/* General slider track styling */
input[type="range"].range-slider {
  -webkit-appearance: none; /* Remove default styling */
  appearance: none;
  width: var(--range-slider-width);
  height: var(--range-slider-height); /* Adjust height for vertical slider */
  background: transparent; /* Make track background transparent */
  outline: none;
  cursor: pointer;
}

/* Styling the track */
input[type="range"].range-slider::-webkit-slider-runnable-track {
  width: 100%;
  height: var(--range-slider-width); /* Track height */
  background: #000; /* Track color */
  border-radius: 8px;
}

input[type="range"].range-slider::-moz-range-track {
  width: 100%;
  height: var(--range-slider-width);
  background: #000;
  border-radius: 8px;
}

/* Styling the thumb (handle) */
input[type="range"].range-slider::-webkit-slider-thumb {
  -webkit-appearance: none;
  appearance: none;
  width: var(--range-slider-width);
  height: var(--range-slider-width);
  background: white;
  border: calc(var(--range-slider-width) / 2) solid white;
  border-radius: 0px;
  box-shadow: none;
  cursor: pointer;
  position: relative;
  box-shadow: 0px 0px 0px var(--range-slider-border) black;
}

input[type="range"].range-slider::-moz-range-thumb {
  width: var(--range-slider-width);
  height: var(--range-slider-width);
  background: white;
  border: calc(var(--range-slider-width) / 2) solid white;
  border-radius: 0px;
  cursor: pointer;
  box-shadow: 0px 0px 0px var(--range-slider-border) black;
}

/* Focus state for accessibility */
input[type="range"].range-slider:focus::-webkit-slider-thumb {
  outline: 1px solid black; /* Add focus ring for accessibility */
}

input[type="range"].range-slider:focus::-moz-range-thumb {
  outline: 1px solid black;
}

<script type="module">
  import Game       from '/wp-content/themes/analogue/assets/Game/Game.js';
  import Playful    from '/wp-content/themes/analogue/assets/Playful/Playful.js';
  import { Utils }  from '/wp-content/themes/analogue/assets/Utils/Utils.js';

  window.utils = Utils;

  // Check if mitt exists before initializing Game and Playful
  if (typeof mitt !== 'undefined') {
    try {
      window.newGame = new Game({ element: document.querySelector('.c-Game') });
      window.newPlayful = new Playful({ element: document.querySelector('.c-Playful') });
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Failed to initialize Game or Playful:", error);
    }
  } else {
    console.warn("mitt is not available. Skipping Game and Playful initialization.");
  }
</script>
<script>

function playfulGame() {

  const isTouchscreen = window.utils.isTouchscreen()

  if(!isTouchscreen) {
    window.newGame.init()
  }

  if(isTouchscreen) {
    window.newPlayful.init()
  }

}

// ===================================================SWUP===================================================//

let isAnimating = false;

const overlayPath = document.querySelector('.overlay__path');

const paths = {
    step1: {
        unfilled: 'M 0 100 V 100 Q 50 100 100 100 V 100 z',
        inBetween: {
            curve1: 'M 0 100 V 50 Q 50 0 100 50 V 100 z',
            curve2: 'M 0 100 V 50 Q 50 100 100 50 V 100 z'
        },
        filled: 'M 0 100 V 0 Q 50 0 100 0 V 100 z',
    },
    step2: {
      filled: 'M 0 0 V 100 Q 50 100 100 100 V 0 z',
      inBetween: {
          curve1: 'M 0 0 V 50 Q 50 0 100 50 V 0 z',
          curve2: 'M 0 0 V 50 Q 50 100 100 50 V 0 z'
      },
      unfilled: 'M 0 0 V 0 Q 50 0 100 0 V 0 z',
  }
};

function pageTransitionIn() {

  if ( isAnimating ) return; 

 gsap.timeline({
    // onComplete: () => isAnimating = false
 })
 .set(overlayPath, {
     attr: { d: paths.step1.unfilled }
 })
 .to(overlayPath, { 
     duration: 0.8,
     ease: 'power4.in',
     attr: { d: paths.step1.inBetween.curve1 }
 }, 0)
 .to(overlayPath, { 
     duration: 0.2,
     ease: 'power1',
     attr: { d: paths.step1.filled }
 });
 isAnimating = true;
 $('body').addClass('transition--start');

}

function pageTransitionOut() {

  if (!isAnimating) return; 

  gsap.timeline({
    onComplete: () => isAnimating = false
  })
  .set(overlayPath, { 
      attr: { d: paths.step2.filled }
  })
  .to(overlayPath, { 
      duration: 0.2,
      ease: 'sine.in',
      attr: { d: paths.step2.inBetween.curve1 }
  })
  .to(overlayPath, { 
      duration: 1,
      ease: 'power4',
      attr: { d: paths.step2.unfilled }
  });

  $('body').removeClass('transition--start');
    
}

// ===================================================
// 1. IN VIEW
// ===================================================

function addClassinView() {
  const inViewport = (elem) => {
    let allElements = $(elem);
    let windowHeight = window.innerHeight * .9;
    const elems = () => {
        for (let i = 0; i < allElements.length; i++) {  //  loop through the sections
            let viewportOffset = allElements[i].getBoundingClientRect();  //  returns the size of an element and its position relative to the viewport
            let top = viewportOffset.top;  //  get the offset top
            if(top < windowHeight){  //  if the top offset is less than the window height
                allElements[i].classList.add('in-view');
            } else{
                //allElements[i].classList.remove('in-view');  //  remove the class
            }
        }
    }
    elems();
    window.addEventListener('scroll', elems);
  }

  //inViewport('section');  //  run the function on all section elements

  inViewport('section');

  //$('section').addClass('in-view');
}

// ===================================================
// 2. ZOOM IMAGE ON SCROLL
// ===================================================

function zoomImageOnScroll() {
    $('.zoom--image').each(function() {
        var rect          = $(this)[0].getBoundingClientRect();
        var windowHeight  = window.innerHeight;
        var elemTop       = windowHeight - rect.top;
        var pct           = (elemTop / windowHeight) * 0.06;

        if (pct < 0) {
            pct = 0;
        }

        var scaleAmount = 1 + pct;

        $(this).find('img').css({
            'transition': 'transform 0.75s ease-out',
            'transform': 'scale(' + scaleAmount + ')'
        });

        setTimeout(() => {
            $(this).find('img').css('transition', 'transform 0s ease-out');
        }, 750);
    });
}

// ===================================================
// 3. BLOCK IN ELEMENTS
// ===================================================

function blockInElements() {

  document.querySelectorAll('.split--into--span').forEach((breakText) => {

    const text = $(this).text;

    // Split the text into individual characters, including spaces
    const characters = [text];

    // Create a new string where each character is wrapped in a <span>
    const wrappedText = characters.map(char => `<span>${char}</span>`).join('');

  });

  document.querySelectorAll('.block--in--text').forEach((introCopy) => {
    
      introCopy.querySelectorAll('.line').forEach((line) => {
          // Get all direct children of the .line element
          const children = Array.from(line.children);
          
          // Hide all children initially by setting display to none
          children.forEach(child => {
              child.style.display = 'none';
          });

          // Shuffle the children in random order
          const shuffledChildren = children.sort(() => Math.random() - 0.5);

          // Show each child sequentially with a 100ms delay
          shuffledChildren.forEach((child, index) => {
              setTimeout(() => {
                  child.style.display = 'inline-block';  // Show the child
              }, index * 200);  // Delay by 100ms for each child
          });
      });
  });
}

// ===================================================
// 4. INERTIA
// ===================================================

function inertia() {
  gsap.registerPlugin(ScrollTrigger, InertiaPlugin, Draggable);

  const items = gsap.utils.toArray(".scroll-item");

  items.forEach((item) => {
      // Create the scroll animation
      gsap.fromTo(
          item,
          { opacity: 1, y: 50 }, // Starting state
          {
              opacity: 1,
              y: 0,
              scrollTrigger: {
                  trigger: item,
                  start: "top 80%", // Trigger when the item enters the viewport
                  end: "top 20%", // End when the item exits the viewport
                  scrub: 0.5, // Control scrubbing speed
                  markers: true, // Show markers for debugging
              },
              inertia: 1, // Increase this value for more inertia
              damping: 0.5, // Lower this value for more floatiness
          }
      );

      // Make the item draggable
      Draggable.create(item, {
          type: "y", // Allow vertical dragging only
          bounds: { minY: 0, maxY: window.innerHeight - item.offsetHeight }, // Restrict drag within the viewport height
          onDrag: function() {
              // Ensure the item doesn't trigger ScrollTrigger while dragging
              ScrollTrigger.update();
          },
          onThrowUpdate: function() {
              // Update the position of the item during the throw
              gsap.to(item, {
                  y: this.y,
                  ease: "power1.out",
                  duration: 1,
              });
          }
      });
  });
  

}

// ===================================================
// 5. TEXT ANIMATION
// ===================================================

function textAnimation() {
  gsap.registerPlugin(ScrollTrigger, SplitText);

  const textElements = document.querySelectorAll(".text-to-animate");

  // Loop through all instances of .text-to-animate
  textElements.forEach(text => {
    // Get the parent section
    const parentSection = text.closest('section');

    // Split text into words, preserving internal HTML structure (including nested elements)
    const split = new SplitText(text, { type: "words" });
    const words = split.words;

    // Wrap each word twice (outer and inner spans), preserving nested elements
    words.forEach((word, index) => {
      const outerSpan = document.createElement('span');
      outerSpan.classList.add('outer');

      const innerSpan = document.createElement('span');
      innerSpan.classList.add('inner');

      // If the word contains child nodes (like <sup>, <span>), move all its children into the inner span
      while (word.firstChild) {
        innerSpan.appendChild(word.firstChild);
      }

      outerSpan.appendChild(innerSpan);
      word.replaceWith(outerSpan);

      // Insert a space after each word except the last one
      if (index < words.length - 1) {
        const space = document.createTextNode(' ');
        outerSpan.parentNode.insertBefore(space, outerSpan.nextSibling);
      }
    });

    // Animate the inner spans
    const innerSpans = text.querySelectorAll('.inner');

    gsap.set(innerSpans, { yPercent: 100 });

    // Check if the element has the class 'delay', and apply delay accordingly
    const animationDelay = text.classList.contains('delay') ? 1.5 : 0;

    gsap.to(innerSpans, {
      yPercent: 0,
      visibility: "visible",
      stagger: 0.025,
      duration: 0.5,
      delay: animationDelay,
      ease: "power2.out",
      scrollTrigger: {
        trigger: parentSection, // Trigger based on the parent section
        start: "top 80%", // Start animation when the section is mostly in view
        toggleActions: "play none none none", // Play the animation only once
        once: true // Only play the animation once
      }
    });
  });
}



// ===================================================GLOBAL===================================================//

// ===================================================
// 1. LENIS
// ===================================================

function lenis() {
  const lenis = new Lenis({
    duration: 1.5,
    easing: function(t){return (t === 1 ? 1 : 1 - Math.pow(2, -10 * t))},
    direction: 'vertical',
    smooth: true,
    smoothTouch: false,
    touchMultiplier: 2,
  })

  //window.lenis = lenis;

  lenis.on('scroll', (e) => {
    // console.log(e)
  })

  function raf(time) {
    lenis.raf(time)
    requestAnimationFrame(raf)
  }

  document.querySelectorAll('a[href^="#"]').forEach(anchor => {

    anchor.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        if($(window).scrollTop() > 60) {
            // $('header').addClass('slideUp');
            // setTimeout(function() { 
            //     $('body').removeClass('slideUp');
            // }, 300);
        }
        lenis.scrollTo(this.getAttribute('href'))
    });
    })
  requestAnimationFrame(raf)
}

// ===================================================
// 2. CURRENT MENU ITEM
// ===================================================

function currentMenuItem() {
  $('.menu .current-menu-item').addClass('active');

  var menuItem = $('.menu a');

  $(menuItem).click(function(){
    $(menuItem).removeClass('active');
    $(this).addClass('active');
  });

}

// ===================================================
// 3. MENU BUTTON
// ===================================================

function menuButton() {
  
  $('.toggle-menu').click(function() {
    $(this).toggleClass('active');
    $('body').toggleClass('menu--active');
    $('#menu').toggleClass('open');
  });

  $('.mobile--menu a, header a').click(function() {
    $('.toggle-menu').removeClass('active');
    $('body').removeClass('menu--active');
    $('#menu').removeClass('open');
  });

  // Function to check browser width and remove classes if width exceeds 1023px
  function checkWidth() {
    if ($(window).width() > 1023) {
      $('body').removeClass('menu--active');
      $('#menu').removeClass('open');
      $('.toggle-menu').removeClass('active');
    }
  }

  // Run checkWidth on window resize
  $(window).resize(function() {
    checkWidth();
  });

  // Run checkWidth on initial load
  checkWidth();
}


// ===================================================
// 4. MENU BUTTON
// ===================================================

function hoverButton() {

  const button = document.querySelector('.button-3d');

  button.addEventListener('click', function() {
      button.classList.add('clicked');
      
      // Optional: remove the 'clicked' class after a short delay (e.g., 1 second)
      setTimeout(() => {
          button.classList.remove('clicked');
      }, 1000); // Adjust duration as needed
  });

  button.addEventListener('mouseleave', function() {
      // Optionally, remove the clicked class when the mouse leaves
      button.classList.remove('clicked');
  });
}

// ===================================================
// 5. CUSTOM CURSOR
// ===================================================

function customCursor() {

  var cursor = document.getElementById('cursor');

  document.addEventListener('mousemove', moveCursor)

  function moveCursor(e) {
    var x = e.clientX;
    var y = e.clientY;
    cursor.style.left = `${x}px`;
    cursor.style.top = `${y}px`;
  }

  var text = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('p'));

  text.forEach(text => {
    text.addEventListener('mousemove', function() {
      cursor.classList.add('hover-cursor');
    })
  //To remove the class when it doesn't hover the text
    text.addEventListener('mouseleave', function () {
      cursor.classList.remove('hover-cursor');
    })
  });

}

  });
}

// ===================================================
// 7. HANDLE RESIZE
// ===================================================

function handleResize() {
  const body = document.body;
  let resizeTimer;

  window.addEventListener('resize', () => {
    // Add the "resizing" class
    body.classList.add('resizing');

    // Clear the previous timer, if any
    clearTimeout(resizeTimer);

    // Set a new timer to remove the "resizing" class after 600 milliseconds
    resizeTimer = setTimeout(() => {
      body.classList.remove('resizing');
    }, 600);
  });
}


// ===================================================
// 8. SCROLL TO TOP
// ===================================================

function scrollTop() {
  // Assuming Lenis is already initialized
  const lenis = new Lenis({
    duration: 1.2, // Control the duration of the scroll (in seconds)
    easing: (t) => Math.min(1, 1.001 - Math.pow(2, -10 * t)), // Optional easing function
  });

  document.querySelector('.scroll-to-top').addEventListener('click', () => {
    lenis.scrollTo(0, { duration: 1.2, easing: (t) => Math.min(1, 1.001 - Math.pow(2, -10 * t)) });
  });

  // Function to keep Lenis running for RAF loop
  function raf(time) {
    lenis.raf(time);
    requestAnimationFrame(raf);
  }

  requestAnimationFrame(raf);

}


// ===================================================PAGES===================================================//

// ===================================================
// Home: 2. CUSTOM VIDEO BUTTON
// ===================================================

function customVideoButton() {
   // Get all videos
   var videos = document.getElementsByClassName("video__play-button");
   var video_fullscreen = document.getElementsByClassName("video__fullscreen-button");
   
   // Loop through all videos
   for (var i = 0; i < videos.length; i++) {
     // On click play button
     videos[i].onclick = function() {
       
       // Find video element
       video          = this.nextElementSibling;
       video_wrapper  = this.parentElement;
       var video_poster   = $(this).parent().parent().find('.poster');


       $(video_poster).css('opacity', 0);
       
       // Play video
       if (video.paused == true) {
         // Play the video
         video.play();
         video.setAttribute('data-state','play');
         video.setAttribute('data-state-reload','false');
         video_wrapper.setAttribute('data-state','play');
 
         // Update the button text to 'Pause'
         // this.innerHTML = "Pause";
         this.setAttribute('data-button-state','play');
         this.setAttribute('data-button-state-reload','false');
       } else {
         // Pause the video
         video.pause();
         video.setAttribute('data-state','pause');
         video_wrapper.setAttribute('data-state','pause');
 
         // Update the button text to 'Play'
         // this.innerHTML = "Play";
         this.setAttribute('data-button-state','pause');
       }
       
       // When video is ended
       video.onended = (event) => {
         // Pause the video
         video.setAttribute('data-state','pause');
         video.setAttribute('data-state-reload','true');
 
         // Update the button text to 'Play'
         this.setAttribute('data-button-state','pause');
         this.setAttribute('data-button-state-reload','true');
       };
       
     }
     
   }
   
   
   // Loop through all videos
   for (var i = 0; i < video_fullscreen.length; i++) {
     // On click play button
     video_fullscreen[i].onclick = function() {
       
       // Find video element
       video = this.nextElementSibling.nextElementSibling;
       
       if (video.mozRequestFullScreen) {
         video.mozRequestFullScreen();
       } else if (video.webkitRequestFullScreen) {
         video.webkitRequestFullScreen();
       }
       
     }
     
   }
 
}

// ===================================================
// Home: 3. POP UP VIDEO
// ===================================================

function popupVideo() {
  const modal = $('.video--modal');
  const modalContentContainer = modal.find('.modal--content');

  if (modalContentContainer.length === 0) {
    modal.append('<div class="modal--content"></div>');
  }

  $('.click--to--play').each(function() {
    $(this).on('click', function() {
      const parentSection = $(this).closest('.relative.row');
      const player = parentSection.find('#player').clone();

      player.attr('id', ''); // Remove duplicate ID
      // Update src with data-src value
      player.find('video, iframe').each(function() {
        const dataSrc = $(this).find('source').attr('data-src');
        if (dataSrc) {
          $(this).attr('src', dataSrc).removeAttr('data-src');
        }
      });

      modal.find('.modal--content').html(player);
      modal.addClass('active');

      // Trigger the video to play once cloned
      const clonedPlayer = modal.find('video').get(0);
      if (clonedPlayer) {
        clonedPlayer.play();
      }

      const originalPlayer = parentSection.find('#player').get(0);
      // if (originalPlayer && !originalPlayer.paused) {
      //   originalPlayer.pause();
      // }
    });
  });

  $('.close--modal').on('click', function() {
    closeModal();
  });

  modal.on('click', function(e) {
    if ($(e.target).hasClass('close--modal--background')) {
      closeModal();
    }
  });

  $(document).on('keydown', function(e) {
    if (e.key === 'Escape' && modal.hasClass('active')) {
      closeModal();
    }
  });

  function closeModal() {
    modal.removeClass('active');
    modal.find('.modal--content').html('');
  }
}

  $('#inflate--button').click (function(){

  });
}

// Work: 1. PROJECT FILTERS
// ===================================================

function projectFilters() {
    const containerEl = document.querySelector('.projects--container');

    if (containerEl) {
        const mixer = mixitup(containerEl, {
            selectors: {
                target: '.project-item'
            },
            animation: {
                duration: 300,
                //effects: 'fade scale(.8)' // Smooth fading and scaling effect on filtering
                effects: 'fade scale(.3)' // Smooth fading and scaling effect on filtering
            }
        });

        // Add a custom listener to the buttons for handling the "active" class
        const allControls = document.querySelectorAll('.filter--button');

        allControls.forEach(control => {
            control.addEventListener('click', () => {
                // Remove the 'active' class from all controls
                allControls.forEach(ctrl => ctrl.classList.remove('active'));

                // Add the 'active' class to the clicked control
                control.classList.add('active');
            });
        });

        // Initial call to set up tooltips
        projectTooltips(); // Call tooltips function on load
    }
}

// ===================================================
// Work: 2. TOOLTIPS
// ===================================================

function projectTooltips() {
    document.querySelectorAll('.project-item').forEach(item => {
        const tooltip = item.querySelector('.tooltip');

        // Ensure the tooltip element exists before adding event listeners
        if (tooltip) {
            item.addEventListener('mouseenter', () => {
                item.classList.add('active'); // Add active class on hover
                tooltip.style.display = 'flex'; // Ensure tooltip is visible when hovered
            });

            item.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => {
                item.classList.remove('active'); // Remove active class on mouse leave
                //tooltip.style.display = 'none'; // Hide tooltip when not hovered
            });

            item.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => {
                // Get the bounding box of the project-item
                const rect = item.getBoundingClientRect();

                // Center the tooltip around the cursor relative to the project-item
                const tooltipWidth = tooltip.offsetWidth;
                const tooltipHeight = tooltip.offsetHeight;
                const offsetX = e.clientX - rect.left; // Cursor X position relative to project-item
                const offsetY = e.clientY - rect.top; // Cursor Y position relative to project-item

                tooltip.style.left = `${offsetX - tooltipWidth / 2}px`;
                tooltip.style.top = `${offsetY - tooltipHeight / 2}px`; // Center vertically within project-item
            });
        }
    });
}

// ===================================================
// Work: 3. FILTER INDICATOR
// ===================================================

function filterIndicator() {
  // File#: _1_morphing-background
  // Usage: codyhouse.co/license
  (function() {
    var MorphBg = function(element) {
      this.element = element;
      this.wrapper = this.element.closest('.js-morph-bg-wrapper');
      this.elementId = this.element.getAttribute('id');
      this.targets = document.querySelectorAll('[data-morph-bg="'+this.elementId+'"]');
      this.bgTargets = [];
      this.action = this.element.getAttribute('data-morph-bg-event');
      this.targetIndex = false;
      this.deafultIndex = false;
      if(!this.action) this.action = 'click';
      initMorphBg(this);
    };

    function initMorphBg(element) {
      // update the element.bgTargets - array of the elements whose size will be used for the morphing transformation
      getBgTargets(element);
      // see if we need to set the element visible
      setInitialState(element);
      // add listeners
      if(element.action == 'click') {
        initClickEvent(element);
      } else {
        initHoverEvent(element);
      }
      // on window resize/fonts loaded - reset background element size
      window.addEventListener('update-morphbg', function(){
        morphBgResize(element);
      });
      window.addEventListener('hide-morphbg', function(){
        morphBgHide(element);
      });
      
    };

    function getBgTargets(element) {
      for(var i = 0; i < element.targets.length; i++) {
        var bgTarget = element.targets[i].querySelector('[data-morph-bg-target]') || element.targets[i];
        element.bgTargets.push(bgTarget);
      }
    };

    function setInitialState(element) {
      for(var i = 0; i < element.targets.length; i++) {
        if(element.targets[i].hasAttribute('data-morph-bg-active')) {
          setPosition(element, i);
          element.deafultIndex = i;
          break;
        }
      }
    };

    function initClickEvent(element) {
      for(var i = 0; i < element.targets.length; i++) {
        (function(i){
          element.targets[i].addEventListener('click', function(event){
            setPosition(element, i);
          })
        })(i);
      }
    };

    function initHoverEvent(element) {
      for(var i = 0; i < element.targets.length; i++) {
        (function(i){
          element.targets[i].addEventListener('mouseenter', function(event){
            setPosition(element, i);
          });
          element.targets[i].addEventListener('mouseleave', function(event){
            resetBgPosition(element, event);
          });
        })(i);
      }

      // if there's [data-morph-bg-preserve] element - detect mouseleave
      var preserveWrapper = element.targets[0].closest('[data-morph-bg-preserve]');
      if(preserveWrapper) {
        preserveWrapper.addEventListener('mouseleave', function(event){
          resetBgPosition(element, event);
        });
      }
    };

    function setPosition(element, index) {
      // get size + position target
      var targetInfo = element.bgTargets[index].getBoundingClientRect(),
        targetRadius = getComputedStyle(element.bgTargets[index]).borderRadius;

      // get the wrapper parent info
      var wrapperInfo = element.wrapper.getBoundingClientRect();

      // modify element position and size
      element.element.style.transform = 'translateX('+(targetInfo.left - wrapperInfo.left)+'px) translateY('+(targetInfo.top - wrapperInfo.top)+'px) translateZ(-0.1px)';
      element.element.style.height = targetInfo.height+'px';
      element.element.style.width = targetInfo.width+'px';

      // modify element radius
      element.element.style.borderRadius = targetRadius;

      // show item
      element.element.classList.add('morph-bg--visible');
      setTimeout(function(){
        if(!element.element.classList.contains('morph-bg--has-transition')) element.element.classList.add('morph-bg--has-transition');
      }, 10);

      // update target index
      element.targetIndex = index;
    };

    function resetBgPosition(element, event) {
      if(event.relatedTarget.closest('[data-morph-bg="'+element.elementId+'"]') || event.relatedTarget.closest('[data-morph-bg-preserve]')) {
        return; // mouse is inside another target
      }
      // check if tehre was a default index
      if(element.deafultIndex !== false) {
        element.targetIndex = element.deafultIndex;
        setPosition(element, element.targetIndex);
        return;
      }
      // if none of the above -> hide bg
      element.element.classList.remove('morph-bg--visible', 'morph-bg--has-transition');
      // reset target index
      element.targetIndex = false;
    };

    function morphBgResize(element) {
      if(element.targetIndex === false) return;
      setPosition(element, element.targetIndex);
      element.element.style.display = '';
    };

    function morphBgHide(element) {
      element.element.style.display = 'none';
    };

    window.MorphBg = MorphBg;

    //initialize the MorphBg objects
    var morphBg = document.getElementsByClassName('js-morph-bg');
    if( morphBg.length > 0 ) {
      for( var i = 0; i < morphBg.length; i++) {
        (function(i){new MorphBg(morphBg[i]);})(i);
      }
    }

    // on window resize - reset morph bg size
    var resizingId = false,
      customEventMorph = new CustomEvent('update-morphbg'),
      customEventHide = new CustomEvent('hide-morphbg');

    window.addEventListener('resize', function() {
      if(!resizingId) doneResizing(customEventHide);
      clearTimeout(resizingId);
      resizingId = setTimeout(function(){
        doneResizing(customEventMorph);
        resizingId = false;
      }, 100);
    });

    // wait for font to be loaded
    if(document.fonts) {
      document.fonts.onloadingdone = function (fontFaceSetEvent) {
        doneResizing(customEventMorph);
      };
      
      document.fonts.ready.then(function() {
        setTimeout(function(){
          doneResizing(customEventMorph);
        }, 300);
      });
    }

    function doneResizing(customEvent) {
      window.dispatchEvent(customEvent);
    };
  }());
}

// ===================================================
// PLAYROOM GRID
// ===================================================

function initializePlayroom() {
  function startPackery() {
    const $grid = $('.playroom--grid');

    // Set the grid to visible before initializing Packery
    $grid.css('display', 'block');

    // Initialize Packery with original order (removed reverse)
    const $items = $grid.find('.playroom--element').get();
    $grid.empty().append($items);

    $grid.packery({
      itemSelector: '.playroom--element',
      gutter: 20,
      transitionDuration: '0s', 
      percentPosition: true
    });

    // Add the 'loaded' class when Packery layout is complete
    $grid.on('layoutComplete', function() {
      $grid.addClass('loaded');
    });

    // Fade in the grid after Packery is initialized
    $grid.fadeIn();
  }

  function initGridItemSpans() {
    const gridItems = document.querySelectorAll('.playroom--element');
    const paddingClasses = [
      'grid--item--padding-a', 'grid--item--padding-b', 'grid--item--padding-c',
      'grid--item--padding-d', 'grid--item--padding-e', 'grid--item--padding-f'
    ];
    const widthClasses = [
      'grid--item--xsmall', 'grid--item--small', 'grid--item--medium',
      'grid--item--large', 'grid--item--xlarge'
    ];

    gridItems.forEach(item => {
      // Remove any existing padding and width classes to prevent duplicates
      paddingClasses.forEach(cls => item.classList.remove(cls));
      widthClasses.forEach(cls => item.classList.remove(cls));

      // Assign one random class from each array
      const randomPaddingClass = paddingClasses[Math.floor(Math.random() * paddingClasses.length)];
      const randomWidthClass = widthClasses[Math.floor(Math.random() * widthClasses.length)];

      item.classList.add(randomPaddingClass);
      item.classList.add(randomWidthClass);
    });
  }

  function setupModalFunctionality() {
    const gridItems = document.querySelectorAll('.playroom--element .grid');
    const zoomContainer = document.getElementById('playroom--zoom--container');
    const zoomMedia = document.getElementById('playroom--zoom--media');

    gridItems.forEach(item => {
      item.addEventListener('click', function() {
        // Add "active" class to clicked element
        item.closest('.playroom--element').classList.add('active');

        // Add "playground--zoom--active" class to body
        document.body.classList.add('playground--zoom--active');

        // Clone media to modal
        cloneMediaToModal(item);
      });
    });

    zoomContainer.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
      if (e.target === zoomContainer) {
        closeModal();
      }
    });

    document.addEventListener('keydown', function(event) {
      if (event.key === 'Escape') {
        closeModal();
      }
    });
  }

  function cloneMediaToModal(item) {
    const zoomMedia = document.getElementById('playroom--zoom--media');
    zoomMedia.innerHTML = '';

    // Check if the clicked item contains a video
    const videoElement = item.querySelector('video');
    const imgElement = item.querySelector('img');

    if (videoElement) {
      // Get the current time of the video before cloning
      const currentTime = videoElement.currentTime;

      // Clone the video element
      const videoClone = videoElement.cloneNode(true);
      videoClone.style.objectFit = 'contain';

      // Append the cloned video to the modal
      zoomMedia.appendChild(videoClone);

      // Wait for the cloned video to be ready before setting the time and playing
      videoClone.addEventListener('loadedmetadata', function() {
        videoClone.currentTime = currentTime; // Set the current time of the cloned video
        videoClone.play(); // Play the video from the current time
      });
    } else if (imgElement) {
      // Clone the image element
      const imgClone = imgElement.cloneNode(true);
      imgClone.style.objectFit = 'contain';

      // Append the cloned image to the modal
      zoomMedia.appendChild(imgClone);
    }
  }

  function closeModal() {
    const zoomContainer = document.getElementById('playroom--zoom--container');
    const zoomMedia = document.getElementById('playroom--zoom--media');

    // Remove the "active" class from all grid elements
    document.querySelectorAll('.playroom--element.active').forEach(activeItem => {
      activeItem.classList.remove('active');
    });

    // Remove "playground--zoom--active" class from body
    document.body.classList.remove('playground--zoom--active');

    // Clear the media from the zoom container
    zoomMedia.innerHTML = '';
  }

  // Initialize all functions
  initGridItemSpans();
  startPackery();
  setupModalFunctionality();

  console.log('v1.2')
}

// ===================================================
// 1. INTRO ANIMATION
// ===================================================

function introAnimation() {
  if (document.querySelector('.intro--active')){
    document.body.scrollTop = document.documentElement.scrollTop = 0;
    $('body').addClass('intro--animating');
    setTimeout(function() { 
      document.body.scrollTop = document.documentElement.scrollTop = 0;
      $('body').removeClass('intro--active');
    }, 300);
    setTimeout(function() {
      $('body').attr('data-lenis-prevent', false);
      $('body').removeClass('intro--incomplete');
    }, 2000);
  }
}

    'https://stg-analogue-staging.kinsta.cloud/wp-content/themes/analogue/img/favicon--02.png',

    'https://stg-analogue-staging.kinsta.cloud/wp-content/themes/analogue/img/favicon--08.png'
  ],
  image_counter = 0; // To keep track of the current image

  setInterval(function() {
      $("link[rel='icon']").remove();
      $("link[rel='shortcut icon']").remove();
      $("head").append('<link rel="icon" href="' + favicon_images[image_counter] + '" type="image/gif">');
      
    // If last image then goto first image
    // Else go to next image    
    if(image_counter == favicon_images.length -1)
          image_counter = 0;
      else
          image_counter++;
  }, 100);

}

// ===================================================
// 3. ANIMATE PLAYROOM MENU ITEM
// ===================================================

function playroomAnimation() {

  function animatePlayroom() {

    $('.main-menu .playroom.menu-item').each(function () {

      var el          = $(this);
      var text        = 'Playroom';
      var characters  = text.split("");

      $(el).text(null);
      
      $.each(characters, function (i, singleChar) {
        el.append("<span class='letter'>" + singleChar + "</span");
      });

    });

  }

  animatePlayroom();

  function addClassPlayroom() {
    $('.main-menu .playroom.menu-item').addClass('animate--playroom');
    setTimeout(function() {
      $('.main-menu .playroom.menu-item').removeClass('animate--playroom');
    }, 4000);
  }

  setInterval(addClassPlayroom,9000);

}

// ===================================================
// 4. FOOTER MARQUEE
// ===================================================

function footerMarquee() {
  gsap.registerPlugin(Observer);

  const scrollingText = gsap.utils.toArray('.footer--marquee .marquee-item-container');

  const tl = horizontalLoop(scrollingText, {
    repeat: -1,
  });

  Observer.create({
    target: window,
    type: "wheel,touch",
    onChangeY(self) {
      let scrollBuffer = 100; // The buffer at the bottom of the page
      let scrollPos = window.scrollY + window.innerHeight;
      let docHeight = document.documentElement.scrollHeight;

      // Only trigger when the user isn't at the very bottom
      if (scrollPos < docHeight - scrollBuffer) {
        let factor = self.deltaY < 0 ? -1 : 1;
        tl.timeScale(factor * 1.5);
      }
    }
  });

  window.addEventListener('resize', () => {
    tl.kill(); // Kill the previous timeline
    horizontalLoop(scrollingText, { repeat: -1 }); // Re-initialize the loop
  });

  /*
  This helper function makes a group of elements animate along the x-axis in a seamless, responsive loop.

  Features:
  - Uses xPercent so that even if the widths change (like if the window gets resized), it should still work in most cases.
  - When each item animates to the left or right enough, it will loop back to the other side
  - Optionally pass in a config object with values like "speed" (default: 1, which travels at roughly 100 pixels per second), paused (boolean),  repeat, reversed, and paddingRight.
  - The returned timeline will have the following methods added to it:
    - next() - animates to the next element using a timeline.tweenTo() which it returns. You can pass in a vars object to control duration, easing, etc.
    - previous() - animates to the previous element using a timeline.tweenTo() which it returns. You can pass in a vars object to control duration, easing, etc.
    - toIndex() - pass in a zero-based index value of the element that it should animate to, and optionally pass in a vars object to control duration, easing, etc. Always goes in the shortest direction
    - current() - returns the current index (if an animation is in-progress, it reflects the final index)
    - times - an Array of the times on the timeline where each element hits the "starting" spot. There's also a label added accordingly, so "label1" is when the 2nd element reaches the start.
  */
  function horizontalLoop(items, config) {
    items = gsap.utils.toArray(items);
    config = config || {};
    let tl = gsap.timeline({repeat: config.repeat, paused: config.paused, defaults: {ease: "none"}, onReverseComplete: () => tl.totalTime(tl.rawTime() + tl.duration() * 100)}),
      length = items.length,
      startX = items[0].offsetLeft,
      times = [],
      widths = [],
      xPercents = [],
      curIndex = 0,
      pixelsPerSecond = (config.speed || 1) * 100,
      snap = config.snap === false ? v => v : gsap.utils.snap(config.snap || 1), // some browsers shift by a pixel to accommodate flex layouts, so for example if width is 20% the first element's width might be 242px, and the next 243px, alternating back and forth. So we snap to 5 percentage points to make things look more natural
      totalWidth, curX, distanceToStart, distanceToLoop, item, i;
    gsap.set(items, { // convert "x" to "xPercent" to make things responsive, and populate the widths/xPercents Arrays to make lookups faster.
      xPercent: (i, el) => {
        let w = widths[i] = parseFloat(gsap.getProperty(el, "width", "px"));
        xPercents[i] = snap(parseFloat(gsap.getProperty(el, "x", "px")) / w * 100 + gsap.getProperty(el, "xPercent"));
        return xPercents[i];
      }
    });
    gsap.set(items, {x: 0});
    totalWidth = items[length-1].offsetLeft + xPercents[length-1] / 100 * widths[length-1] - startX + items[length-1].offsetWidth * gsap.getProperty(items[length-1], "scaleX") + (parseFloat(config.paddingRight) || 0);
    for (i = 0; i < length; i++) {
      item = items[i];
      curX = xPercents[i] / 100 * widths[i];
      distanceToStart = item.offsetLeft + curX - startX;
      distanceToLoop = distanceToStart + widths[i] * gsap.getProperty(item, "scaleX");
      tl.to(item, {xPercent: snap((curX - distanceToLoop) / widths[i] * 100), duration: distanceToLoop / pixelsPerSecond}, 0)
        .fromTo(item, {xPercent: snap((curX - distanceToLoop + totalWidth) / widths[i] * 100)}, {xPercent: xPercents[i], duration: (curX - distanceToLoop + totalWidth - curX) / pixelsPerSecond, immediateRender: false}, distanceToLoop / pixelsPerSecond)
        .add("label" + i, distanceToStart / pixelsPerSecond);
      times[i] = distanceToStart / pixelsPerSecond;
    }
    function toIndex(index, vars) {
      vars = vars || {};
      (Math.abs(index - curIndex) > length / 2) && (index += index > curIndex ? -length : length); // always go in the shortest direction
      let newIndex = gsap.utils.wrap(0, length, index),
        time = times[newIndex];
      if (time > tl.time() !== index > curIndex) { // if we're wrapping the timeline's playhead, make the proper adjustments
        vars.modifiers = {time: gsap.utils.wrap(0, tl.duration())};
        time += tl.duration() * (index > curIndex ? 1 : -1);
      }
      curIndex = newIndex;
      vars.overwrite = true;
      return tl.tweenTo(time, vars);
    }
    tl.next = vars => toIndex(curIndex+1, vars);
    tl.previous = vars => toIndex(curIndex-1, vars);
    tl.current = () => curIndex;
    tl.toIndex = (index, vars) => toIndex(index, vars);
    tl.times = times;
    tl.progress(1, true).progress(0, true); // pre-render for performance
    if (config.reversed) {
      tl.vars.onReverseComplete();
      tl.reverse();
    }
    return tl;
  }
}

function clientsCarousel() {

 // Loop through each .clients--carousel container
 $('.clients--carousel').each(function() {
    var $carouselContainer = $(this); // current instance of .clients--carousel
    
    // Initialize Flickity for the main carousel within this container
    var $carouselMain = $carouselContainer.find('.carousel-main').flickity({
      pageDots: false,
      prevNextButtons: false,
      selectedAttraction: 0.1,
      friction: 1,
      fade: true
    });

    // Initialize Flickity for the nav carousel within this container
    var $carouselNav = $carouselContainer.find('.carousel-nav').flickity({
      asNavFor: $carouselContainer.find('.carousel-main')[0], // use the main carousel in this container
      contain: true,
      pageDots: false,
      prevNextButtons: false
    });

    // Select main carousel slide on nav hover
    $carouselNav.on('mouseover', '.carousel-cell', function(event) {
      var index = $(event.currentTarget).index();
      $carouselMain.flickity('select', index);
    });
  });

}

// PAGE: HOME - DRAGGABLE ELEMENTS
// ===================================================

function draggableElements() {
  document.querySelectorAll('.draggable--container').forEach(($container) => {
    const $elements = $container.querySelectorAll(".drag-me"); // Select all drag-me elements

    if ($elements.length > 0) { // Check if there are elements
      $elements.forEach(($element) => { // Loop through each drag-me element
        Draggable.create($element, {
          bounds: $container,
          edgeResistance: 0.75,
          type: "y,x",
          inertia: true

        });
      });
    } else {
      //console.log('no element');
    }
  });

  document.querySelectorAll('.draggable--container').forEach(($container) => {
    const $elements = $container.querySelectorAll(".drag-and-spin"); // Select all drag-me elements

    if ($elements.length > 0) { // Check if there are elements
      $elements.forEach(($element) => { // Loop through each drag-me element
        Draggable.create($element, {
          bounds: $container,
          edgeResistance: 0.75,
          type: "y,x",
          inertia: true,

          onDrag: function() {
            // Rotate the element while dragging
            gsap.set(this.target, { rotation: this.x * 0.5 });
          }

        });
      });
    } else {
      //console.log('no element');
    }
  });

}

// ===================================================
// PAGE: HOME - REVIEWS
// ===================================================

function reviews() {

  const reviewsContainer = document.querySelector('.reviews--container');
  const reviews = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.review--element'));
  let seenReviews = new Set(); // Keep track of seen reviews

  // Hide all but 4 reviews initially
  reviews.forEach((review, index) => {
      if (index >= 4) {
          review.classList.add('hidden--review');
      }
  });

  // Function to hide a review and show the next unseen one
  function hideReviewAndShowUnseen(currentReview) {
      // Hide the current review
      currentReview.classList.add('hidden--review');

      // Mark the current review as seen
      seenReviews.add(currentReview);

      // Get all hidden reviews that haven't been seen yet
      const unseenReviews = reviews.filter(review => 
          review.classList.contains('hidden--review') && !seenReviews.has(review)
      );

      // If no unseen reviews left, reset the seen reviews
      if (unseenReviews.length === 0) {
          seenReviews.clear(); // Reset seen reviews
      }

      // Get the updated list of unseen reviews after potential reset
      const nextUnseenReviews = reviews.filter(review => 
          review.classList.contains('hidden--review') && !seenReviews.has(review)
      );

      // Unhide the next unseen review
      if (nextUnseenReviews.length > 0) {
          let randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * nextUnseenReviews.length);
          let reviewToUnhide = nextUnseenReviews[randomIndex];

          if (reviewToUnhide) {
              // Remove 'hidden--review' class
              reviewToUnhide.classList.remove('hidden--review');

              // Remove transform
              //reviewToUnhide.style.transform = '';

              // Assign random positions between 10% and 60%
              let randomLeft = Math.random() * (40 - 10) + 10;
              let randomTop = Math.random() * (40 - 10) + 10;
              reviewToUnhide.style.left = `${randomLeft}%`;
              reviewToUnhide.style.top = `${randomTop}%`;

              // Apply animation delay for the revealed review
              reviewToUnhide.style.animationDelay = '1s';
              reviewToUnhide.style.webkitAnimationDelay = '1s'; // For older WebKit browsers
          }
      }
  }

  // Add event listeners to control buttons
  const controls = document.querySelectorAll('.review--control');
  controls.forEach(control => {
      control.addEventListener('click', function() {
          const parentReview = this.closest('.review--element');
          hideReviewAndShowUnseen(parentReview);
      });
  });

}

function projectsCarousel() {

  var galleryElems = document.querySelectorAll('.carousel--projects');

for (var i = 0, len = galleryElems.length; i < len; i++) {
    var galleryElem = galleryElems[i];
    var flkty = new Flickity(galleryElem, {
        pageDots: false,
        percentPosition: true,
        prevNextButtons: true,
        wrapAround: false,
        draggable: true,
        autoPlay: false,
        adaptiveHeight: true,
        groupCells: true,
        pauseAutoPlayOnHover: false,
        freeScroll: false,
        contain: true,
        cellAlign: 'left'
    });

    // Disable link interactions during dragging
    flkty.on('dragStart', function () {
        galleryElem.style.pointerEvents = 'none';
    });

    flkty.on('dragEnd', function () {
        setTimeout(() => {
            galleryElem.style.pointerEvents = 'auto';
        }, 50);
    });
}


}


// ===================================================
// PAGE: STUDIO - IMAGE STACKER
// ===================================================


function imageStacker() {
  // body element
  const body = document.body;

  // helper functions
  const MathUtils = {
      // linear interpolation
      lerp: (a, b, n) => (1 - n) * a + n * b,
      // distance between two points
      distance: (x1, y1, x2, y2) => Math.hypot(x2 - x1, y2 - y1)
  };

  // get the mouse or touch position
  const getPointerPos = (ev) => {
      let posx = 0;
      let posy = 0;
      if (ev.touches && ev.touches.length > 0) {
          // If it's a touch event
          posx = ev.touches[0].pageX;
          posy = ev.touches[0].pageY;
      } else if (ev.pageX || ev.pageY) {
          // If it's a mouse event
          posx = ev.pageX;
          posy = ev.pageY;
      } else if (ev.clientX || ev.clientY) {
          posx = ev.clientX + body.scrollLeft;
          posy = ev.clientY + body.scrollTop;
      }
      return { x: posx, y: posy };
  };

  // mousePos: current mouse position
  // cacheMousePos: previous mouse position
  // lastMousePos: last recorded mouse position (at the time the last image was shown)
  let mousePos = lastMousePos = cacheMousePos = { x: 0, y: 0 };

  // images container
  const stackerElement = document.querySelector('.image--stacker');
  let isPointerOverStacker = false;

  // Function to check if the pointer is currently inside the element on load
  const checkPointerInside = () => {
      const rect = stackerElement.getBoundingClientRect();
      if (
          mousePos.x >= rect.left &&
          mousePos.x <= rect.right &&
          mousePos.y >= rect.top &&
          mousePos.y <= rect.bottom
      ) {
          isPointerOverStacker = true;
      }
  };

  // Update pointer state
  stackerElement.addEventListener('mouseenter', (ev) => {
      isPointerOverStacker = true;
      mousePos = getPointerPos(ev); // Capture pointer position when entering
  });

  stackerElement.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => {
      isPointerOverStacker = false;
  });

  window.addEventListener('mousemove', (ev) => {
      mousePos = getPointerPos(ev);
      if (isPointerOverStacker === false) {
          checkPointerInside(); // Check if mouse is over element after movement
      }
  });

  // Add touch event listeners for mobile devices
  stackerElement.addEventListener('touchstart', (ev) => {
      isPointerOverStacker = true;
      mousePos = getPointerPos(ev); // Capture touch position when starting
      ev.preventDefault(); // Prevent page scroll on touch start
  });

  stackerElement.addEventListener('touchend', () => {
      isPointerOverStacker = false;
  });

  window.addEventListener('touchmove', (ev) => {
      mousePos = getPointerPos(ev);
      ev.preventDefault(); // Prevent page scroll on touch move
      if (isPointerOverStacker === false) {
          checkPointerInside(); // Check if touch is over element after movement
      }
  });

  // Initial check to see if the pointer is already inside the element
  checkPointerInside();

  class Image {
      constructor(el) {
          this.DOM = { el: el };
          // image default styles
          this.defaultStyle = {
              x: 0,
              y: 0,
              opacity: 0
          };
          // get sizes/position
          this.getRect();
          // init/bind events
          this.initEvents();
      }
      initEvents() {
          // on resize get updated sizes/position
          window.addEventListener('resize', () => this.resize());
      }
      resize() {
          // reset styles
          gsap.set(this.DOM.el, this.defaultStyle);
          // get sizes/position
          this.getRect();
      }
      getRect() {
          this.rect = this.DOM.el.getBoundingClientRect();
      }
      isActive() {
          // check if image is animating or if it's visible
          return gsap.isTweening(this.DOM.el) || this.DOM.el.style.opacity != 0;
      }
  }

  class ImageTrail {
      constructor() {
          // images container
          this.DOM = { content: document.querySelector('.stacker--content') };
          // array of Image objs, one per image element
          this.images = [];
          [...this.DOM.content.querySelectorAll('img')].forEach(img => this.images.push(new Image(img)));
          // total number of images
          this.imagesTotal = this.images.length;
          // upcoming image index
          this.imgPosition = 0;
          // zIndex value to apply to the upcoming image
          this.zIndexVal = 1;
          // mouse distance required to show the next image
          this.threshold = 100;
          // render the images
          requestAnimationFrame(() => this.render());
      }
      render() {
          // If the pointer is not over the stacker element, skip rendering
          if (!isPointerOverStacker) {
              requestAnimationFrame(() => this.render());
              return;
          }

          // get distance between the current mouse position and the position of the previous image
          let distance = MathUtils.distance(mousePos.x, mousePos.y, lastMousePos.x, lastMousePos.y);
          // cache previous mouse position
          cacheMousePos.x = MathUtils.lerp(cacheMousePos.x || mousePos.x, mousePos.x, 0.1);
          cacheMousePos.y = MathUtils.lerp(cacheMousePos.y || mousePos.y, mousePos.y, 0.1);

          // if the pointer moved more than [this.threshold] then show the next image
          if (distance > this.threshold) {
              this.showNextImage();

              ++this.zIndexVal;
              this.imgPosition = this.imgPosition < this.imagesTotal - 1 ? this.imgPosition + 1 : 0;

              lastMousePos = mousePos;
          }

          // check when pointer stops and all images are inactive (not visible and not animating)
          let isIdle = true;
          for (let img of this.images) {
              if (img.isActive()) {
                  isIdle = false;
                  break;
              }
          }
          // reset z-index initial value
          if (isIdle && this.zIndexVal !== 1) {
              this.zIndexVal = 1;
          }

          // loop..
          requestAnimationFrame(() => this.render());
      }
      showNextImage() {
          // show image at position [this.imgPosition]
          const img = this.images[this.imgPosition];
          // kill any tween on the image
          gsap.killTweensOf(img.DOM.el);

          gsap.timeline()
              // show the image
              .set(img.DOM.el, {
                  opacity: 1,
                  scale: 1,
                  zIndex: this.zIndexVal,
                  x: cacheMousePos.x - img.rect.width / 2,
                  y: cacheMousePos.y - img.rect.height / 2
              })
              // animate position
              .to(img.DOM.el, {
                  duration: 1.8,
                  ease: "expo.out",
                  x: mousePos.x - img.rect.width / 2,
                  y: mousePos.y - img.rect.height / 2
              })
              // then make it disappear
              .to(img.DOM.el, {
                  duration: 0,
                  ease: "power1.out",
                  opacity: 0
              }, 0.8)
              // scale down the image
              .to(img.DOM.el, {
                  duration: 0,
                  ease: "quint.inOut",
                  scale: 2
              }, 0.8);
      }
  }
  new ImageTrail();
}


// ===================================================
// PAGE: STUDIO - CLONE IMAGE
// ===================================================

function createAndUpdateImage() {
  // Get the container to append the new image
  const container = document.querySelector('.stacker--content');
    if (!container) return;

    // Create a new image element
    let newImage = document.querySelector('.stacker--image--random');
    if (!newImage) {
        newImage = document.createElement('img');
        newImage.classList.add('stacker--image--random');
        container.appendChild(newImage);
    }

    // Get the list of all images in the container
    const allImages = [...container.querySelectorAll('img.stacker--image')];
    if (allImages.length === 0) return;

    // Set the src of the new image to the next image in the container (in order)
    let nextImageIndex = (newImage.dataset.currentIndex ? parseInt(newImage.dataset.currentIndex) + 1 : 0) % allImages.length;
    newImage.src = allImages[nextImageIndex].src;
    newImage.dataset.currentIndex = nextImageIndex;

    // Randomize the position within the container
    const containerRect = container.getBoundingClientRect();
    const randomX = Math.random() * (containerRect.width - newImage.width);
    const randomY = Math.random() * (containerRect.height - newImage.height);

    // Set the position of the new image
    newImage.style.position = 'absolute';
    newImage.style.left = `${randomX}px`;
    newImage.style.top = `${randomY}px`;
    newImage.style.opacity = 1;

    // Display the image for 1 second, then move and update the source
    setTimeout(() => {
        newImage.style.opacity = 0;
        setTimeout(() => {
            createAndUpdateImage();
        }, 100);
    }, 600);
}



// ===================================================
// PAGE: STUDIO - TEAM
// ===================================================

function teamPhotos() {

!function(e){"undefined"==typeof module?this.charming=e:module.exports=e}(function(e,n){"use strict";n=n||{};var t=n.tagName||"span",o=null!=n.classPrefix?n.classPrefix:"char",r=1,a=function(e){for(var n=e.parentNode,a=e.nodeValue,c=a.length,l=-1;++l<c;){var d=document.createElement(t);o&&(d.className=o+r,r++),d.appendChild(document.createTextNode(a[l])),n.insertBefore(d,e)}n.removeChild(e)};return function c(e){for(var n=[].slice.call(e.childNodes),t=n.length,o=-1;++o<t;)c(n[o]);e.nodeType===Node.TEXT_NODE&&a(e)}(e),e});

  const mapNumber = (X,A,B,C,D) => (X-A)*(D-C)/(B-A)+C;
  // from http://www.quirksmode.org/js/events_properties.html#position
const getMousePos = (e) => {
      let posx = 0;
      let posy = 0;
  if (!e) e = window.event;
  if (e.pageX || e.pageY) {
          posx = e.pageX;
    posy = e.pageY;
  }
  else if (e.clientX || e.clientY) {
    posx = e.clientX + document.body.scrollLeft + document.documentElement.scrollLeft;
    posy = e.clientY + document.body.scrollTop + document.documentElement.scrollTop;
  }
      return { x : posx, y : posy }
  }
  // Generate a random float.
  const getRandomFloat = (min, max) => (Math.random() * (max - min) + min).toFixed(2);

  /**
   * One class per effect. 
   * Lots of code is repeated, so that single effects can be easily used. 
   */

  // Effect 1
  class HoverImgFx1 {
      constructor(el) {
          this.DOM = { el: el };
          
          // Parse the image URLs from the data attribute and store them in an array
          this.images = el.dataset.imgs.split(',');
          this.currentImageIndex = 0;

          this.DOM.reveal = document.createElement('div');
          this.DOM.reveal.className = 'hover-reveal';
          this.DOM.reveal.innerHTML = `<div class="hover-reveal__inner"><div class="hover-reveal__img"></div></div>`;
          this.DOM.el.appendChild(this.DOM.reveal);
          
          this.DOM.revealInner = this.DOM.reveal.querySelector('.hover-reveal__inner');
          this.DOM.revealImg = this.DOM.revealInner.querySelector('.hover-reveal__img');
          
          this.initEvents();
      }

      initEvents() {
          this.positionElement = (ev) => {
              const mousePos = getMousePos(ev);
              const docScrolls = {
                  left: document.body.scrollLeft + document.documentElement.scrollLeft,
                  top: document.body.scrollTop + document.documentElement.scrollTop
              };
              this.DOM.reveal.style.top = `${mousePos.y + 20 - docScrolls.top}px`;
              this.DOM.reveal.style.left = `${mousePos.x + 20 - docScrolls.left}px`;
          };

          this.mouseenterFn = (ev) => {
              this.updateImage(); // Set the next image on each hover
              this.positionElement(ev);
              this.showImage();
          };
          
          this.mousemoveFn = ev => requestAnimationFrame(() => {
              this.positionElement(ev);
          });

          this.mouseleaveFn = () => {
              this.hideImage();
          };
          
          this.DOM.el.addEventListener('mouseenter', this.mouseenterFn);
          this.DOM.el.addEventListener('mousemove', this.mousemoveFn);
          this.DOM.el.addEventListener('mouseleave', this.mouseleaveFn);
      }

      updateImage() {
          // Cycle through images and set the current one
          this.currentImageIndex = (this.currentImageIndex + 1) % this.images.length;
          this.DOM.revealImg.style.backgroundImage = `url(${this.images[this.currentImageIndex]})`;
      }

      showImage() {
          // Set z-index and fade in
          TweenMax.killTweensOf(this.DOM.reveal);
          TweenMax.set(this.DOM.el, { zIndex: 1000 });
          TweenMax.set(this.DOM.reveal, { opacity: 1, display: 'block' });
          TweenMax.to(this.DOM.reveal, 0.1, { opacity: 1 });
      }

      hideImage() {
          // Fade out and reset z-index after fade completes
          TweenMax.killTweensOf(this.DOM.reveal);
          TweenMax.to(this.DOM.reveal, 0.01, {
              opacity: 1,
              onComplete: () => {
                  TweenMax.set(this.DOM.reveal, { display: 'none' });
                  TweenMax.set(this.DOM.el, { zIndex: '' }); // Reset z-index
              }
          });
      }
  }

  [...document.querySelectorAll('[data-fx="1"] > .team--member, .team--member[data-fx="1"]')].forEach(link => new HoverImgFx1(link));

  //========MOBILE========//
  $('.team--member').on('click', function() {
    // Remove 'active' class from all siblings
      $(this).siblings().removeClass('active');

      // Add 'active' class to the clicked element
      $(this).addClass('active');
  });

  // Event listener for closing the image (e.g., clicking outside or a close button)
  $(document).on('click', function(event) {
      if (!$(event.target).closest('.team--member').length) {
          // Remove 'active' class from all '.team--member' elements
          $('.team--member').removeClass('active');
      }
  });

  // Remove active classes and close overlays on window resize
  window.addEventListener('resize', () => {
      $('.team--member').removeClass('active');
      const overlay = document.querySelector('.team-photo-overlay');
      if (overlay) {
          overlay.parentNode.removeChild(overlay);
      }
  });
}

// ===================================================
// PAGE: STUDIO - TEAM MOBILE
// ===================================================

function teamPhotosMobile() {
  const teamMembers = document.querySelectorAll('.team--member');

  teamMembers.forEach(member => {
      member.addEventListener('click', () => {
          const imageUrl = member.getAttribute('data-mobile');
          if (imageUrl) {
              // Create an overlay element
              const overlay = document.createElement('div');
              overlay.className = 'team-photo-overlay'; // Add class to overlay for easy targeting
              overlay.style.position = 'fixed';
              overlay.style.top = '0';
              overlay.style.left = '0';
              overlay.style.width = '100%';
              overlay.style.height = '100%';
              overlay.style.backgroundColor = 'transparent';
              overlay.style.display = 'flex';
              overlay.style.justifyContent = 'center';
              overlay.style.alignItems = 'center';
              overlay.style.zIndex = '2001';

              // Create an image element
              const image = document.createElement('img');
              image.src = imageUrl;
              image.style.width = '80%';
              image.style.height = 'auto';
              image.style.cursor = 'pointer';
              image.style.transform = 'scale(0)';
              image.style.transition = 'transform 0.3s ease';

              // Append image to overlay
              overlay.appendChild(image);

              // Append overlay to body
              document.body.appendChild(overlay);

              // Trigger scale up animation
              requestAnimationFrame(() => {
                  image.style.transform = 'scale(1)';
              });

              // Add click event to close the overlay
              overlay.addEventListener('click', () => {
                  image.style.transform = 'scale(0)';
                  image.addEventListener('transitionend', () => {
                      document.body.removeChild(overlay);
                  }, { once: true });
              });
          }
      });
  });

  // Remove active classes and close overlays on window resize
  window.addEventListener('resize', () => {
      teamMembers.forEach(member => member.classList.remove('active'));
      const overlay = document.querySelector('.team-photo-overlay');
      if (overlay) {
          overlay.parentNode.removeChild(overlay);
      }
  });
}

// PAGE: CONNECT - CONTROLS
