// Define a global flag to track the mute state
let isMuted = false;

function ctrlVolume() {
  const volumeControlButton = document.querySelector('.ctrl--volume');
  const allAudioElements = document.querySelectorAll('audio');
  
  // Event listener for the volume control button
  volumeControlButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
    // Toggle the .active class on the button
    $(this).toggleClass('active');
    console.log('click');

    // Toggle the mute flag
    isMuted = !isMuted;

    // Mute or unmute all audio elements based on the flag
    allAudioElements.forEach(audio => {
      audio.muted = isMuted;
    });
  });
}





function ctrlClock() {
    const clocks = document.getElementsByClassName("clock");

    function updateClocks() {
        for (let clock of clocks) {
            // You can add timezone logic here if needed
            //let timezone = clock.dataset.timezone;

            const date = new Date();
            
            // Format the date
            const year = String(date.getFullYear()).slice(-2); // Last 2 digits of the year
            const month = String(date.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0'); // Month is 0-indexed, so add 1
            const day = String(date.getDate()).padStart(2, '0'); // Two-digit day
            
            // Format the time
            const time = date.toLocaleTimeString("en-US", {
                hour: "2-digit",
                minute: "2-digit",
                hour12: true
            }).toUpperCase(); // Ensures AM/PM is uppercase

            // Combine date and time
            const formattedDateTime = `${day}.${month}.${year}   ${time}`;

            // Update the clock element's text content
            clock.textContent = formattedDateTime;
        }
    }

    setInterval(updateClocks, 10000);
    updateClocks();
}
function ctrlDial() {
    const dial = document.querySelector('.dial');
    const sound = document.getElementById('ctrl--tuning');
    let isDragging = false;
    let currentAngle = 0;
    let totalRotation = 0; // Track accumulated rotation
    let previousAngle = 0;
    let soundDuration = 0;

    // Ensure the sound plays continuously in the background
    sound.loop = true;  // Set the sound to loop
    sound.muted = true; // Start with the sound muted

    // Event listeners for mouse actions
    dial.addEventListener('mousedown', startDragging);
    document.addEventListener('mousemove', rotateDial);
    document.addEventListener('mouseup', stopDragging);

    // Get the sound's duration when it loads
    sound.addEventListener('loadedmetadata', () => {
        soundDuration = sound.duration; // Get the duration of the sound
    });

    function startDragging(e) {
        isDragging = true;
        previousAngle = getAngle(e.pageX, e.pageY);

        // Only unmute and play the sound if not muted
        if (!isMuted) {
            sound.muted = false;
            sound.play();
        }
    }

    function rotateDial(e) {
        if (isDragging) {
            const newAngle = getAngle(e.pageX, e.pageY);
            let rotationAngle = newAngle - previousAngle;
            
            // Normalize the rotation to prevent flipping between 0 and 360 degrees
            if (rotationAngle > 180) rotationAngle -= 360;
            if (rotationAngle < -180) rotationAngle += 360;

            totalRotation += rotationAngle;  // Accumulate the total rotation
            currentAngle = (totalRotation % 360 + 360) % 360;  // Keep current angle between 0 and 360
            
            dial.style.transform = `rotate(${currentAngle}deg)`;
            previousAngle = newAngle;

            // Calculate the percentage of the rotation based on the total rotation
            const rotationPercentage = (currentAngle / 360);
            
            // Map the rotation percentage to the sound's current time
            sound.currentTime = rotationPercentage * soundDuration;
        }
    }

    function stopDragging() {
        isDragging = false;

        // Mute the sound when dragging stops
        if (!isMuted) {
            sound.muted = true;
        }
    }

    function getAngle(x, y) {
        const rect = dial.getBoundingClientRect();
        const centerX = rect.left + rect.width / 2;
        const centerY = rect.top + rect.height / 2;
        const radians = Math.atan2(y - centerY, x - centerX);
        const degrees = (radians * 180) / Math.PI;
        return degrees;
    }
}
function ctrlSample() {
    // Array of audio file paths
    const audioClips = [
        '/audio/ctrl--sample--1.mp3',
        '/audio/ctrl--sample--2.mp3',
        '/audio/ctrl--sample--3.mp3'
    ];

    // Function to play a random audio clip
    function playRandomAudio() {
        if (!isMuted) {
            const randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * audioClips.length);
            const audio = new Audio(audioClips[randomIndex]);
            audio.play();
        }
    }

    // Event listener for button click
    document.getElementById('ctrl--button--sample').addEventListener('click', playRandomAudio);
}
function ctrlDrum() {
    // Array of audio file paths for each sound in the pattern
    const pattern = [
        '/audio/ctrl--CB.mp3', // Pong
        '/audio/ctrl--OH.mp3', // Hi-Hat
        '/audio/ctrl--CP.mp3', // Clap
        '/audio/ctrl--OH.mp3',
        '/audio/ctrl--BD.mp3', // Bass Drum
        '/audio/ctrl--OH.mp3', // Hi-Hat
        '/audio/ctrl--CP.mp3', // Clap
        '/audio/ctrl--OH.mp3',
        '/audio/ctrl--BD.mp3', // Bass Drum
        '/audio/ctrl--OH.mp3', // Hi-Hat
        '/audio/ctrl--CP.mp3', // Clap
        '/audio/ctrl--HH.mp3',
        '/audio/ctrl--BD.mp3', // Bass Drum
        '/audio/ctrl--OH.mp3', // Hi-Hat
        '/audio/ctrl--CP.mp3', // Clap
        '/audio/ctrl--OH.mp3',
        '/audio/ctrl--BD.mp3', // Bass Drum
        '/audio/ctrl--OH.mp3', // Hi-Hat
        '/audio/ctrl--CP.mp3', // Clap
        '/audio/ctrl--OH.mp3'
    ];

    let currentIndex = 0; // To keep track of the current sound in the pattern

    // Function to play audio at a specific index in the pattern
    function playSound(index) {
        if (!isMuted) {
            const audio = new Audio(pattern[index]);
            audio.play();
        }
    }

    // Function to handle the click event and play the next sound in the pattern
    function playNextSound() {
        playSound(currentIndex); // Play the sound at the current index
        currentIndex++; // Move to the next sound in the pattern

        // Reset index to 0 if we've reached the end of the pattern (loop back to the start)
        if (currentIndex >= pattern.length) {
            currentIndex = 0;
        }
    }

    // Event listener for button click
    document.getElementById('ctrl--button--drum').addEventListener('click', playNextSound);
}
function ctrlRange() {
  const slider = document.getElementById('color-slider');
  const root = document.documentElement;

  slider.addEventListener('input', (event) => {
    const value = event.target.value;

    let color;
    if (value == 0) {
      color = 'black'; // Set color to black when slider is at the bottom
    } else {
      const hue = Math.round((value / 100) * 360);
      color = `hsl(${hue}, 100%, 50%)`;
    }

    root.style.setProperty('--screen-background', color);
  });
}
function updateRangeSliderHeight() {
  const container = document.querySelector('.ctrl--slider--container');

  if (container) {
    // Calculate 80% of the container's height
    const containerHeight = container.offsetHeight;
    const sliderHeight = containerHeight * 0.75;

    // Set the inline CSS variable
    container.style.setProperty('--range-slider-height', `${sliderHeight}px`);
  }
}
function ctrlRec() {
  let mediaRecorder;
  let audioChunks = [];
  let recordedAudioBuffer = null;
  let isRecording = false;
  let playbackRate = 1.0; // Default playback rate

  const recordButton = document.querySelector(".ctrl--button--record");
  const playButton = document.querySelector(".ctrl--button--play");
  const slider = document.getElementById('color-slider');

  recordButton.addEventListener("click", () => {
    if (!isRecording) {
      startRecording();
    } else {
      stopRecording();
    }
  });

  playButton.addEventListener("click", () => {
    if (recordedAudioBuffer) {
      playRecordingWithEffects();
    }
  });

  slider.addEventListener('input', (event) => {
    // Update playback rate based on slider value (0.5x to 2x speed)
    playbackRate = 0.5 + (event.target.value / 100) * 1.5; // Range from 0.5 to 2.0
  });

  function startRecording() {
    navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({ audio: true })
      .then(stream => {
        mediaRecorder = new MediaRecorder(stream);
        mediaRecorder.ondataavailable = event => {
          audioChunks.push(event.data);
        };
        mediaRecorder.onstop = () => {
          const audioBlob = new Blob(audioChunks, { type: 'audio/wav' });
          const audioUrl = URL.createObjectURL(audioBlob);

          const audioContext = new (window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext)();
          fetch(audioUrl)
            .then(response => response.arrayBuffer())
            .then(data => audioContext.decodeAudioData(data))
            .then(buffer => {
              recordedAudioBuffer = buffer;
            });

          audioChunks = [];
        };

        // Store the media stream in the mediaRecorder instance
        mediaRecorder.stream = stream;

        mediaRecorder.start();
        isRecording = true;

        // Update button styles
        recordButton.style.backgroundColor = "red";
        recordButton.querySelector("div").innerText = "STOP";
      })
      .catch(error => {
        console.error("Error accessing microphone: ", error);
      });
  }

  function stopRecording() {
    mediaRecorder.stop();
    isRecording = false;

    // Stop all tracks on the media stream to release the microphone
    mediaRecorder.stream.getTracks().forEach(track => track.stop());

    // Reset button styles
    recordButton.style.backgroundColor = "";
    recordButton.querySelector("div").innerText = "REC";
  }

  function playRecordingWithEffects() {
    const audioContext = new (window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext)();
    
    // Create source from the recorded audio buffer
    const source = audioContext.createBufferSource();
    source.buffer = recordedAudioBuffer;

    // Set playback rate based on slider value
    source.playbackRate.value = playbackRate;

    // Distortion (WaveShaper Node)
    const distortion = audioContext.createWaveShaper();
    function makeDistortionCurve(amount) {
      const n_samples = 44100;
      const curve = new Float32Array(n_samples);
      const deg = Math.PI / 180;
      let x;
      for (let i = 0; i < n_samples; ++i) {
        x = (i * 2) / n_samples - 1;
        curve[i] = ((3 + amount) * x * 20 * deg) / (Math.PI + amount * Math.abs(x));
      }
      return curve;
    }
    distortion.curve = makeDistortionCurve(400);
    distortion.oversample = '4x';

    // Delay Nodes (Echo Effect)
    const delay1 = audioContext.createDelay();
    delay1.delayTime.value = 0.2; // 200 ms delay for the first echo

    const delay2 = audioContext.createDelay();
    delay2.delayTime.value = 0.4; // 400 ms delay for the second echo

    const feedbackGain1 = audioContext.createGain();
    feedbackGain1.gain.value = 0.4; // Control feedback intensity for delay 1

    const feedbackGain2 = audioContext.createGain();
    feedbackGain2.gain.value = 0.3; // Control feedback intensity for delay 2

    // Gain Node for controlling volume
    const gainNode = audioContext.createGain();
    gainNode.gain.value = 0.8;

    // Connect nodes
    source.connect(distortion);
    distortion.connect(delay1);
    delay1.connect(feedbackGain1);
    feedbackGain1.connect(delay1); // Feedback loop for first delay

    delay1.connect(delay2);
    delay2.connect(feedbackGain2);
    feedbackGain2.connect(delay2); // Feedback loop for second delay

    delay2.connect(gainNode);
    gainNode.connect(audioContext.destination);

    // Start playback
    source.start();
  }

}
function ctrlNews() {
  document.getElementById('scroll-to-footer').addEventListener('click', function() {
      const footer = document.getElementById('footer');
      if (footer) {
          footer.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });
      }
      console.log('footer')
  });
}
function ctrlSmiley() {
    document.querySelector('.ctrl--button--smiley').addEventListener('click', function() {
      const icons = document.querySelectorAll('.ctrl--icon');
      const activeIcon = document.querySelector('.ctrl--icon.active');

      // Convert NodeList to an array and filter out the current active icon
      const selectableIcons = Array.from(icons).filter(icon => icon !== activeIcon);

      let nextIcon;

      // Ensure a new icon is selected
      do {
          nextIcon = selectableIcons[Math.floor(Math.random() * selectableIcons.length)];
      } while (nextIcon === activeIcon);

      // Remove active class from current active icon
      if (activeIcon) {
          activeIcon.classList.remove('active');
      }

      // Add active class to the new icon
      nextIcon.classList.add('active');
  });

}
function connectControls() {

  ctrlVolume();
  ctrlClock();
  ctrlDial();
  ctrlSample();
  ctrlDrum();
  ctrlRange();
  ctrlRec();
  ctrlNews();
  ctrlSmiley();

  // Initial setup
  updateRangeSliderHeight();

  // Update on window resize
  window.addEventListener('resize', updateRangeSliderHeight);
}


// ===================================================
// INLINE MAILCHIMP VALIDATION
// ===================================================
 
        
function mailchimpInline() {
          
  $("#mc-embedded-subscribe-form").submit(function(e){
    e.preventDefault();
    submitSubscribeForm($("#mc-embedded-subscribe-form"), $("#subscribe-result-form"), $("#subscribe-result-error"));
  });

  var subscriptionSuccess     = $('body').data('subscription');
  var subscribedAlready       = $('body').data('subscribed-already');
  var subscriptionFailure     = $('body').data('subscription-failure');

  function submitSubscribeForm($form, $resultElement, $resultFailure) {
    $.ajax({
      type: "GET",
      url: $form.attr("action"),
      data: $form.serialize(),
      cache: false,
      dataType: "jsonp",
      jsonp: "c",
      contentType: "application/json; charset=utf-8",

      error: function(error){},

      success: function(data){
        if (data.result != "success") {

          var message = "<span class='failure'>" + subscriptionFailure + "</span>";

          if (data.msg && data.msg.indexOf("already subscribed") >= 0) {
            message = subscribedAlready;
          }

          $resultFailure.html(message);

        } else {

          $resultElement.html("<span class='success rounded--medium'>" + subscriptionSuccess + "</h3>");
          $form.css({
            display: 'none'
          });

          $resultFailure.html(null);

        }
      }
    });
  }
}

// ===================================================
// SECTION – ACCORDION JOBS
// ===================================================

function accordionSmall() {
  document.querySelectorAll('.accordion-header').forEach((header) => {
    header.addEventListener('click', () => {
        const accordionItem = header.closest('.accordion-item');
        const content = accordionItem.querySelector('.accordion-content');

        if (accordionItem.classList.contains('active')) {
            // Close the accordion
            content.style.height = `${content.scrollHeight}px`; // Set the current height
            requestAnimationFrame(() => {
                content.style.height = '0';
            });
            accordionItem.classList.remove('active');
        } else {
            // Open the current accordion
            content.style.height = `${content.scrollHeight}px`;
            accordionItem.classList.add('active');

            // Remove the inline height after the transition ends
            content.addEventListener(
                'transitionend',
                () => {
                    if (accordionItem.classList.contains('active')) {
                        content.style.height = 'auto';
                    }
                },
                { once: true }
            );
        }
    });
});


}

function initialLoad() {

    //============ RESET ============//

    // SCROLL TO TOP
    window.scrollTo(0, 0);
    document.body.scrollTop = document.documentElement.scrollTop = 0;

    // ADD INITIAL LOAD
    $('body').addClass('initial-load');


    //============ GLOBAL FUNCTIONS ============//

    // 1. LENIS
    lenis();

    // 2. CURRENT MENU ITEM 
    currentMenuItem();

    // 3. MENU BUTTON
    menuButton();

    // 4. 3D BUTTON
    hoverButton();

    // 5. CURSOR
    //    customCursor();

    // 7. HANDLE RESIZE
    handleResize();

    // 8. SCROLL TO TOP
    scrollTop();

    //============---- FEATURES ============---//

    // 1. INTRO ANIMATION
    introAnimation();

    // 2. FAVICON
    animatedFavicon();
    
    // 3. PLAYROOM
    $( document ).ready(function() {
      playroomAnimation();
    });

    // 4. GAME
    $( document ).ready(function() {
      playfulGame();
    });

}

function init() {


    document.body.scrollTop = document.documentElement.scrollTop = 0;

    document.body.classList.remove('.inflate--active');

    //============ SWUP ============//

    // 1. TRANSITION
    setTimeout(function() { pageTransitionOut(); }, 300);

    //============ GLOBAL FUNCTIONS ============//

    // 1. LENIS
    observer.observe();

    // 4. INERTIA
    inertia();
    
    //splitText();

    // 4. FOOTER MARQUEE
    if (document.querySelector('.footer--marquee'))    { footerMarquee(); }

    // 5. MAILCHIMP
    if (document.querySelector('#mc_embed_signup'))    { mailchimpInline(); }


    //============ TRANSITIONS ============//

    // 1. IN VIEW
    addClassinView();

    // 2. ZOOM IMAGE ON SCROLL
    if (document.querySelector('.zoom--image'))             { zoomImageOnScroll(); $(window).on('scroll resize', zoomImageOnScroll); }

    // 3. BLOCK IN TEXT
    //if (document.querySelector('.block--in--text'))         { revealChildrenInRandomOrder();  }

    // 4. TEXT ANIMATION
    if (document.querySelector('.text-to-animate'))         { textAnimation();  }

    //============ PAGES ============//

    // 1. HOME
    if (document.querySelector('.draggable--container'))    { draggableElements();    }
    if (document.querySelector('.reviews--container'))      { reviews();              }
    if (document.querySelector('#inflate--button'))         { inflateButton();        }
    if (document.querySelector('.click--to--play'))         { popupVideo();           }
    if (document.querySelector('.carousel--projects'))      { projectsCarousel();     }

    // 2. WORK
    if (document.querySelector('.projects--filters'))       { projectFilters();       }
    if (document.querySelector('.projects--filters'))       { filterIndicator();      }
    if (document.querySelector('.project-item'))            { projectTooltips();      }
    if (document.querySelector('.carousel'))                { carousels();            }

    // 3. SERVICES
    if (document.querySelector('.clients--carousel'))       { clientsCarousel();      }

    // 4. STUDIO
    if (document.querySelector('.image--stacker'))          { imageStacker();         }
    if (document.querySelector('.image--stacker'))          { createAndUpdateImage();     }
    // if (document.querySelector('.image--stacker'))          { stackerMobile();        }
    if (document.querySelector('.team--profiles'))          { teamPhotos();           }
    if (document.querySelector('.team--profiles'))          { teamPhotosMobile()      }
    if (document.querySelector('.video__play-button'))      { customVideoButton();    }
    if (document.querySelector('.accordion-section')) 	    { accordionSmall();		 		}

    // 5. PLAYROOM
    if (document.querySelector('.playroom--grid') && window.innerWidth >= 768) { initializePlayroom(); }

    // 6. CONNECT
    if (document.querySelector('.ctrl--wrapper'))           { connectControls();       }

    // 7. PROJECT
    if (document.querySelector('.plyr--player'))            { plyr();                 }

}
